ccg(1,
 fc('S[wq]/PP',
  lf(1,1,'S[wq]/S[q]'),
  fc('S[q]/PP',
   fa('S[q]/(S[b]\NP)',
    lf(1,2,'(S[q]/(S[b]\NP))/NP'),
    ba('NP',
     fa('NP[nb]',
      lf(1,3,'NP[nb]/N'),
      lf(1,4,'N')),
     fa('NP\NP',
      lf(1,5,'(NP\NP)/NP'),
      fa('NP[nb]',
       lf(1,6,'NP[nb]/N'),
       lf(1,7,'N'))))),
   fa('(S[b]\NP)/PP',
    lf(1,8,'((S[b]\NP)/PP)/PP'),
    fa('PP',
     lf(1,9,'PP/NP'),
     rp('NP',
      ba('NP',
       fa('NP[nb]',
        lf(1,10,'NP[nb]/N'),
        lf(1,11,'N')),
       fa('NP\NP',
        lf(1,12,'(NP\NP)/NP'),
        fa('NP[nb]',
         lf(1,13,'NP[nb]/N'),
         lf(1,14,'N')))),
      lf(1,15,'.'))))))).

ccg(8,
 fc('S[wq]/(S[b]\NP)',
  lf(8,1,'S[wq]/S[q]'),
  fa('S[q]/(S[b]\NP)',
   lf(8,2,'(S[q]/(S[b]\NP))/NP'),
   rp('NP',
    ba('NP',
     lex('N','NP',
      fa('N',
       lf(8,3,'N/N'),
       lf(8,4,'N'))),
     lex('S[dcl]/NP','NP\NP',
      fc('S[dcl]/NP',
       tr('S[X]/(S[X]\NP)',
        ba('NP',
         lex('N','NP',
          lf(8,5,'N')),
         fa('NP\NP',
          lf(8,6,'(NP\NP)/NP'),
          lex('N','NP',
           lf(8,7,'N'))))),
       bx('(S[dcl]\NP)/NP',
        bx('(S[dcl]\NP)/NP',
         lf(8,8,'((S[dcl]\NP)/PP)/NP'),
         tr('(S[X]\NP)\((S[X]\NP)/PP)',
          fa('PP',
           lf(8,9,'PP/NP'),
           ba('NP',
            lf(8,10,'NP'),
            fa('NP\NP',
             lf(8,11,'(NP\NP)/NP'),
             fa('NP[nb]',
              lf(8,12,'NP[nb]/N'),
              lf(8,13,'N'))))))),
        fa('(S[X]\NP)\(S[X]\NP)',
         lf(8,14,'((S[X]\NP)\(S[X]\NP))/NP'),
         lex('N','NP',
          lf(8,15,'N'))))))),
    lf(8,16,'.'))))).
